Task instruction sent to agent 
# [Kubernetes] Add NoScheduleNoTraffic Taint Effect

**Repository:** kubernetes/kubernetes  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** big_code_feature
**Task Type:** Feature Implementation - Large Codebase

**Reference:** [Trevor's Big Code Research](../../../docs/TREVOR_RESEARCH_DEC2025.md#2-kubernetes-noschedulenotraffic-taint-effect)

## Description

Implement a new Node taint effect called `NoScheduleNoTraffic` that:
1. **Prevents new pods from being scheduled** (like `NoSchedule`)
2. **Removes the node from Service EndpointSlices** (affects traffic routing)
3. **Does NOT evict existing pods** (unlike `NoExecute`)

This is a distinct effect from existing `NoSchedule` (which doesn't affect traffic) and `NoExecute` (which evicts pods).

## Task

This task requires implementing code changes to add `NoScheduleNoTraffic` support.

### Required Implementation

Address implementation concerns in these areas:

1. **Taint Effect Constants & Enums**:
   - Find where taint effects (`NoSchedule`, `NoExecute`, etc.) are defined as constants
   - Add `NoScheduleNoTraffic` alongside them

2. **Pod Admission Logic**:
   - Find the scheduler/admission controller that checks taint effects
   - Add logic to reject pods on nodes with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint
   - Must handle toleration matching for the new effect

3. **Endpoint Slice Update Logic**:
   - Find where service endpoints are updated based on taint effects
   - Add logic to exclude nodes with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` from EndpointSlices
   - Ensure traffic doesn't route to tainted nodes

4. **Node Controller Logic**:
   - Verify taint effect handling in node lifecycle
   - Ensure `NoScheduleNoTraffic` doesn't trigger pod eviction (unlike `NoExecute`)

5. **Tests & Validation**:
   - Add test cases for the new taint effect
   - Verify scheduling is blocked
   - Verify traffic is redirected away from tainted nodes
   - Verify pods are NOT evicted

### Implementation Steps

1. **Understand taint effect architecture**:
   - Find all definitions of taint effects constants
   - Find where `NoSchedule` and `NoExecute` are used
   - Understand the tolerance matching algorithm
   - Find endpoint slice controller logic

2. **Implement the new effect**:
   - Add `NoScheduleNoTraffic` as a new taint effect constant
   - Update all scheduler/admission checks to handle the new effect
   - Modify endpoint slice controller to exclude nodes with the new effect
   - Add Go tests covering the new behavior

3. **Verify no regressions**:
   - Existing taint effects still work correctly
   - Scheduling tests pass
   - Endpoint controller tests pass
   - Node lifecycle tests pass

## Success Criteria

[x] New taint effect `NoScheduleNoTraffic` is defined and used throughout codebase  
[x] Pods cannot be scheduled on nodes with the taint (unless they have matching toleration)  
[x] Nodes with the taint are excluded from Service EndpointSlices  
[x] Existing pods on nodes with the taint are NOT evicted  
[x] All Kubernetes tests pass  
[x] Code follows Kubernetes conventions  

## Testing

```bash
make test
```

  3509→const (
  3510→	// Do not allow new pods to schedule onto the node unless they tolerate the taint,
  3511→	// but allow all pods submitted to Kubelet without going through the scheduler
  3512→	// to start, and allow all already-running pods to continue running.
  3513→	// Enforced by the scheduler.
  3514→	TaintEffectNoSchedule TaintEffect = "NoSchedule"
  3515→	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but the scheduler tries not to schedule
  3516→	// new pods onto the node, rather than prohibiting new pods from scheduling
  3517→	// onto the node entirely. Enforced by the scheduler.
  3518→	TaintEffectPreferNoSchedule TaintEffect = "PreferNoSchedule"
  3519→	// NOT YET IMPLEMENTED. TODO: Uncomment field once it is implemented.
  3520→	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but additionally do not allow pods submitted to
  3521→	// Kubelet without going through the scheduler to start.
  3522→	// Enforced by Kubelet and the scheduler.
  3523→	// TaintEffectNoScheduleNoAdmit TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoAdmit"
  3524→
  3525→	// Evict any already-running pods that do not tolerate the taint.
  3526→	// Currently enforced by NodeController.
  3527→	TaintEffectNoExecute TaintEffect = "NoExecute"

    17→package v1

    19→import "fmt"
    20→
    21→// MatchTaint checks if the taint matches taintToMatch. Taints are unique by key:effect,
    22→// if the two taints have same key:effect, regard as they match.
    23→func (t *Taint) MatchTaint(taintToMatch *Taint) bool {
    24→	return t.Key == taintToMatch.Key && t.Effect == taintToMatch.Effect
    25→}
    26→
    27→// taint.ToString() converts taint struct to string in format '<key>=<value>:<effect>', '<key>=<value>:', '<key>:<effect>', or '<key>'.
    28→func (t *Taint) ToString() string {
    29→	if len(t.Effect) == 0 {
    30→		if len(t.Value) == 0 {
    31→			return fmt.Sprintf("%v", t.Key)
    32→		}
    33→		return fmt.Sprintf("%v=%v:", t.Key, t.Value)
    34→	}
    35→	if len(t.Value) == 0 {
    36→		return fmt.Sprintf("%v:%v", t.Key, t.Effect)
    37→	}
    38→	return fmt.Sprintf("%v=%v:%v", t.Key, t.Value, t.Effect)
    39→}

    15→*/
    16→
    17→package helper
    18→
    19→import v1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
    20→
    21→// DoNotScheduleTaintsFilterFunc returns the filter function that can
    22→// filter out the node taints that reject scheduling Pod on a Node.
    23→func DoNotScheduleTaintsFilterFunc() func(t *v1.Taint) bool {
    24→	return func(t *v1.Taint) bool {
    25→		// PodToleratesNodeTaints is only interested in NoSchedule and NoExecute taints.
    26→		return t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoSchedule || t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoExecute
    27→	}
    28→}

## Summary of Taint Effects Usage in Kubernetes Codebase

I've completed a comprehensive search of the Kubernetes codebase for taint effect usage. Here are my findings:

### 1. **API Definitions**
- **File**: `/workspace/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go`
  - Defines `TaintEffectNoSchedule`, `TaintEffectPreferNoSchedule`, and `TaintEffectNoExecute`
  - Line 3514-3527: Taint effect constant definitions
  - `NoSchedule`: Prevents new pod scheduling (enforced by scheduler)
  - `PreferNoSchedule`: Soft scheduling constraint (scheduler tries to avoid)
  - `NoExecute`: Evicts running pods that don't tolerate (enforced by NodeController/taint manager)

- **File**: `/workspace/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/taint.go`
  - Implements `MatchTaint()` function to compare taints by key and effect
  - Implements `ToString()` for string representation

### 2. **Scheduler Logic** 
- **`/workspace/pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/helper/taint.go`**
  - `DoNotScheduleTaintsFilterFunc()` filters for `TaintEffectNoSchedule` and `TaintEffectNoExecute` only
  - Used by scheduler plugins to determine which taints block pod scheduling

- **`/workspace/pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/tainttoleration/taint_toleration.go`**
  - Implements `TaintToleration` plugin as FilterPlugin, PreScorePlugin, and ScorePlugin
  - `Filter()`: Checks pod tolerations against node taints (line 67)
  - `Score()`: Counts intolerable `PreferNoSchedule` taints (line 152)
  - Validates tolerations match taint effects

- **`/workspace/pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go`**
  - Checks if pods tolerate node taints before scheduling

- **`/workspace/pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/podtopologyspread/common.go`**
  - Filters nodes based on tai

    18→
    19→import v1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
    20→
    21→// DoNotScheduleTaintsFilterFunc returns the filter function that can
    22→// filter out the node taints that reject scheduling Pod on a Node.
    23→func DoNotScheduleTaintsFilterFunc() func(t *v1.Taint) bool {
    24→	return func(t *v1.Taint) bool {
    25→		// PodToleratesNodeTaints is only interested in NoSchedule and NoExecute taints.
    26→		return t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoSchedule || t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoExecute
    27→	}
    28→}

  3163→// TaintEffect defines the effects of Taint
  3164→type TaintEffect string
  3165→
  3166→// These are valid values for TaintEffect
  3167→const (
  3168→	// Do not allow new pods to schedule onto the node unless they tolerate the taint,
  3169→	// but allow all pods submitted to Kubelet without going through the scheduler
  3170→	// to start, and allow all already-running pods to continue running.
  3171→	// Enforced by the scheduler.
  3172→	TaintEffectNoSchedule TaintEffect = "NoSchedule"
  3173→	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but the scheduler tries not to schedule
  3174→	// new pods onto the node, rather than prohibiting new pods from scheduling
  3175→	// onto the node entirely. Enforced by the scheduler.
  3176→	TaintEffectPreferNoSchedule TaintEffect = "PreferNoSchedule"
  3177→	// NOT YET IMPLEMENTED. TODO: Uncomment field once it is implemented.
  3178→	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but additionally do not allow pods submitted to
  3179→	// Kubelet without going through the scheduler to start.
  3180→	// Enforced by Kubelet and the scheduler.
  3181→	// TaintEffectNoScheduleNoAdmit TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoAdmit"
  3182→
  3183→	// Evict any already-running pods that do not tolerate the taint.
  3184→	// Currently enforced by NodeController.
  3185→	TaintEffectNoExecute TaintEffect = "NoExecute"
  3186→)
  3187→

  3190→// the triple <key,value,effect> using the matching operator <operator>.
  3191→type Toleration struct {
  3192→	// Key is the taint key that the toleration applies to. Empty means match all taint keys.
  3193→	// If the ke

   254→// isNodeReady returns true if a node is ready; false otherwise.
   255→func isNodeReady(node *v1.Node) bool {
   256→	for _, c := range node.Status.Conditions {
   257→		if c.Type == v1.NodeReady {
   258→			return c.Status == v1.ConditionTrue
   259→		}
   260→	}
   261→	return false
   262→}
   263→
   264→// numReadyEndpoints returns the number of Endpoints that are ready from the
   265→// specified list.
   266→func numReadyEndpoints(endpoints []discovery.Endpoint) int {
   267→	var total int
   268→	for _, ep := range endpoints {
   269→		if ep.Conditions.Ready != nil && *ep.Conditions.Ready {
   270→			total++
   271→		}
   272→	}
   273→	return total
   274→}
   275→
   276→// EndpointReady returns true if an Endpoint has the Ready condition set to
   277→// true.
   278→func EndpointReady(endpoint discovery.Endpoint) bool {
   279→	return endpoint.Conditions.Ready != nil && *endpoint.Conditions.Ready
   280→}

const (
	// NamespaceDefault means the object is in the default namespace which is applied when not specified by clients
	NamespaceDefault string = "default"
	// NamespaceAll is the default argument to specify on a context when you want to list or filter resources across all namespaces
	NamespaceAll string = ""
	// NamespaceNodeLease is the namespace where we place node lease objects (used for node heartbeats)
	NamespaceNodeLease string = "kube-node-lease"
)

// Volume represents a named volume in a pod that may be accessed by any container in the pod.
type Volume struct {
	// name of the volume.
	// Must be a DNS_LABEL and unique within the pod.
	// More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#names
	Name string `json:"name" protobuf:"bytes,1,opt,name=name"`
	// volumeSource represents the location and type of the mounted volume.
	// If not specified, the Volume is implied to be an EmptyDir.
	// This implied behavior is deprecated and will be removed in a future version.
	VolumeSource `json:",inline" protobuf:"bytes,2,opt,name=volumeSource"`
}

  3506→// +enum
  3507→type TaintEffect string
  3508→
  3509→const (
  3510→	// Do not allow new pods to schedule onto the node unless they tolerate the taint,
  3511→	// but allow all pods submitted to Kubelet without going through the scheduler
  3512→	// to start, and allow all already-running pods to continue running.
  3513→	// Enforced by the scheduler.
  3514→	TaintEffectNoSchedule TaintEffect = "NoSchedule"
  3515→	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but the scheduler tries not to schedule
  3516→	// new pods onto the node, rather than prohibiting new pods from scheduling
  3517→	// onto the node entirely. Enforced by the scheduler.
  3518→	TaintEffectPreferNoSchedule TaintEffect = "PreferNoSchedule"
  3519→	// NOT YET IMPLEMENTED. TODO: Uncomment field once it is implemented.
  3520→	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but additionally do not allow pods submitted to
  3521→	// Kubelet without going through the scheduler to start.
  3522→	// Enforced by Kubelet and the scheduler.
  3523→	// TaintEffectNoScheduleNoAdmit TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoAdmit"
  3524→

  3527→	TaintEffectNoExecute TaintEffect = "NoExecute"

With the current\n\t// rate-limiter in use (1s*2^(numRetries-1)) the following numbers represent\n\t// the sequence of delays between successive queuings of a service.\n\t//\n\t// 1s, 2s, 4s, 8s, 16s, 32s, 64s, 128s, 256s, 512s, 1000s (max)\n\tmaxRetries = 15\n\n\t// endpointSliceChangeMinSyncDelay indicates the minimum delay before\n\t// queuing a syncService call after an EndpointSlice changes. If\n\t// endpointUpdatesBatchPeriod is greater than this value, it will be used\n\t// instead. This helps batch processing of changes to multiple\n\t// EndpointSlices.\n\tendpointSliceChangeMinSyncDelay = 1 * time.Second\n\n\t// defaultSyncBackOff is the default backoff period for syncService calls.\n\tdefaultSyncBackOff = 1 * time.Second\n\t// maxSyncBackOff is the max backoff period for syncService calls.\n\tmaxSyncBackOff = 1000 * time.Second\n\n\t// controllerName is a unique value used with LabelManagedBy to indicated\n\t// the component managing an EndpointSlice.\n\tcontrollerName = \"endpointslice-controller.k8s.io\"\n)\n\n// NewController creates and initializes a new Controller\nfunc NewController(ctx context.Context, podInformer coreinformers.PodInformer,\n\tserviceInformer coreinformers.ServiceInformer,\n\tnodeInformer coreinformers.NodeInformer,\n\tendpointSliceInformer discoveryinformers.EndpointSliceInformer,\n\tmaxEndpointsPerSlice int32,\n\tclient clientset.Interface,\n\tendpointUpdatesBatchPeriod time.Duration,\n) *Controller {\n\tbroadcaster := record.NewBroadcaster(record.WithContext(ctx))\n\trecorder := broadcaster.NewRecorder(scheme.Scheme, v1.EventSource{Component: \"endpoint-slice-controller\"})\n\n\tendpointslicemetrics.RegisterMetrics()\n\n\tc := &Controller{\n\t\tclient: client,\n\t\t// This is similar to the DefaultControllerRateLimiter, just with a\n\t\t// significantly higher default backoff (1s vs 5ms). This controller\n\t\t// processes events that can require significant EndpointSlice changes,\n\t\t// such as an update to a Service or Deployment. If no EndpointSlice can be found, a nil pointer\n// will be returned.\nfunc getSliceToFill(endpointSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice, numEndpoints, maxEndpoints int) (slice *discovery.EndpointSlice) {\n\tclosestDiff := maxEndpoints\n\tvar closestSlice *discovery.EndpointSlice\n\tfor _, endpointSlice := range endpointSlices {\n\t\tcurrentDiff := maxEndpoints - (numEndpoints + len(endpointSlice.Endpoints))\n\t\tif currentDiff >= 0 && currentDiff < closestDiff {\n\t\t\tclosestDiff = currentDiff\n\t\t\tclosestSlice = endpointSlice\n\t\t\tif closestDiff == 0 {\n\t\t\t\treturn closestSlice\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn closestSlice\n}\n\n// addTriggerTimeAnnotation adds a triggerTime annotation to an EndpointSlice\nfunc addTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice 1. EDIT /workspace/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go
Before
const (
	// Do not allow new pods to schedule onto the node unless they tolerate the taint,
	// but allow all pods submitted to Kubelet without going through the scheduler
	// to start, and allow all already-running pods to continue running.
	// Enforced by the scheduler.
	TaintEffectNoSchedule TaintEffect = "NoSchedule"
	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but the scheduler tries not to schedule
	// new pods onto the node, rather than prohibiting new pods from scheduling
	// onto the node entirely. Enforced by the scheduler.
	TaintEffectPreferNoSchedule TaintEffect = "PreferNoSchedule"
	// NOT YET IMPLEMENTED. TODO: Uncomment field once it is implemented.
	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but additionally do not allow pods submitted to
	// Kubelet without going through the scheduler to start.
	// Enforced by Kubelet and the scheduler.
	// TaintEffectNoScheduleNoAdmit TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoAdmit"

	// Evict any already-running pods that do not tolerate the taint.
	// Currently enforced by NodeController.
	TaintEffectNoExecute TaintEffect = "NoExecute"
)
After
const (
	// Do not allow new pods to schedule onto the node unless they tolerate the taint,
	// but allow all pods submitted to Kubelet without going through the scheduler
	// to start, and allow all already-running pods to continue running.
	// Enforced by the scheduler.
	TaintEffectNoSchedule TaintEffect = "NoSchedule"
	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but the scheduler tries not to schedule
	// new pods onto the node, rather than prohibiting new pods from scheduling
	// onto the node entirely. Enforced by the scheduler.
	TaintEffectPreferNoSchedule TaintEffect = "PreferNoSchedule"
	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but additionally evict the node from traffic.
	// Do not allow new pods to schedule onto the node unless they tolerate the taint,
	// and remove the node from the Service EndpointSlices, but allow all already-running
	// pods to continue running.
	// Enforced by the scheduler and the EndpointSlice controller.
	TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoTraffic"
	// NOT YET IMPLEMENTED. TODO: Uncomment field once it is implemented.
	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but additionally do not allow pods submitted to
	// Kubelet without going through the scheduler to start.
	// Enforced by Kubelet and the scheduler.
	// TaintEffectNoScheduleNoAdmit TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoAdmit"

	// Evict any already-running pods that do not tolerate the taint.
	// Currently enforced by NodeController.
	TaintEffectNoExecute TaintEffect = "NoExecute"
)

import os

# Read the file
with open('/workspace/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Find the position to insert the new taint effect
old_text = '''	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but additionally do not allow pods submitted to
	// Kubelet without going through the scheduler to start.
	// Enforced by Kubelet and the scheduler.
	// TaintEffectNoScheduleNoAdmit TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoAdmit"

	// Evict any already-running pods that do not tolerate the taint.
	// Currently enforced by NodeController.
	TaintEffectNoExecute TaintEffect = "NoExecute"'''

new_text = '''	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but additionally evict the node from traffic.
	// Do not allow new pods to schedule onto the node unless they tolerate the taint,
	// and remove the node from the Service EndpointSlices, but allow all already-running
	// pods to continue running.
	// Enforced by the scheduler and the EndpointSlice controller.
	TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoTraffic"
	// NOT YET IMPLEMENTED. TODO: Uncomment field once it is implemented.
	// Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but additionally do not allow pods submitted to
	// Kubelet without going through the scheduler to start.
	// Enforced by Kubelet and the scheduler.
	// TaintEffectNoScheduleNoAdmit TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoAdmit"

	// Evict any already-running pods that do not tolerate the taint.
	// Currently enforced by NodeController.
	TaintEffectNoExecute TaintEffect = "NoExecute"'''

# Replace the text
if old_text in content:
    new_content = content.replace(old_text, new_text)
    # Write the file
    with open('/workspace/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go', 'w') as f:
        f.write(new_content)
    print("File updated successfully")
else:
    print("ERROR: Could not find the text to replace")
    print("Looking for:", repr(old_text[:50]))
